Oracle Database Server = Instance + Database 

Lab1 - DEVDB
Lab2 - TESTDB

Instance = Memory + BG Process 
Memory = PGA + SGA 

PGA - 1
SGA - 3

SGA 
- SP, DBC, LBC
- LP, JP, SP

Select 
Insert - create 
Update 
Delet

BG Process 
- Mondatory - PMON, SMON, DBWR, LGWR, CKPT
- Non-Mandatory - arch, reco

Database
Datafiles 
- system 
- sysaux
- undo
- temp
- user/apps 

password 
spfile/pfile 
alert & trace 
archive logs 
CT
Redo 



spfile / pfile 
===============
$ORACLE_HOME/dbs 
spfileDEVDB.ora - binary 
initDEVDB.ora - text file 

CT:
===
binary file 
/u01/app/oracle/oradata/DEVDB/controlfile/o1_mf_l3spnmkq_.ctl
/u01/app/oracle/fast_recovery_area/DEVDB/controlfile/o1_mf_l3spnmlt_.ctl

DB infomration 
Datafile , Redo , Name, When DB create, SCN
